13:["$","p","p-0",{"data-indent":"2em","children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":"Shader（着色器）"}]," 是用于图形渲染的程序，用于描述如何在 GPU（图形处理单元）上处理图形数据。着色器是现代图形学的重要组成部分，允许开发者对 3D 图形、动画和效果进行高效且灵活的控制。"]}]
14:["$","h2","h2-0",{"id":"shader-的分类","children":"Shader 的分类"}]
15:["$","p","p-1",{"data-indent":"2em","children":"根据执行阶段的不同，Shader 主要分为以下几类："}]
16:["$","ol","ol-0",{"children":["\n",["$","li","li-0",{"children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":"顶点着色器（Vertex Shader）"}],"\n",["$","ul","ul-0",{"children":["\n",["$","li","li-0",{"children":"作用：处理顶点数据（如位置、法线、纹理坐标）。"}],"\n",["$","li","li-1",{"children":"功能：负责将顶点从模型空间变换到屏幕空间，同时可以传递数据给后续阶段（如纹理坐标等）。"}],"\n",["$","li","li-2",{"children":"示例用途：旋转、缩放、位移顶点。"}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-1",{"children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":"片段着色器（Fragment Shader）"}],"\n",["$","ul","ul-0",{"children":["\n",["$","li","li-0",{"children":"作用：处理屏幕上每个像素的颜色。"}],"\n",["$","li","li-1",{"children":"功能：负责计算像素的最终颜色值，可以应用光照、纹理、透明度等。"}],"\n",["$","li","li-2",{"children":"示例用途：实现材质效果、光照模型、后处理效果。"}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-2",{"children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":"几何着色器（Geometry Shader）"}],"\n",["$","ul","ul-0",{"children":["\n",["$","li","li-0",{"children":"作用：可以生成或修改几何体。"}],"\n",["$","li","li-1",{"children":"功能：处理图元（如点、线、三角形）的形状，可以创建额外的顶点或完全改变输入的图元。"}],"\n",["$","li","li-2",{"children":"示例用途：实现细节层次（LOD）、生成草丛或粒子系统。"}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-3",{"children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":"计算着色器（Compute Shader）"}],"\n",["$","ul","ul-0",{"children":["\n",["$","li","li-0",{"children":"作用：不限定于图形渲染，用于在 GPU 上执行通用计算任务。"}],"\n",["$","li","li-1",{"children":"功能：可以用于并行计算，如模拟物理效果、处理大规模数据。"}],"\n",["$","li","li-2",{"children":"示例用途：粒子系统模拟、图像处理。"}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-4",{"children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":"曲面细分着色器（Tessellation Shader）"}],"\n",["$","ul","ul-0",{"children":["\n",["$","li","li-0",{"children":["包括：\n",["$","ul","ul-0",{"children":["\n",["$","li","li-0",{"children":["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":"细分控制着色器（Tessellation Control Shader）"}]}],"\n",["$","li","li-1",{"children":["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":"细分评价着色器（Tessellation Evaluation Shader）"}]}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-1",{"children":"功能：用于细分曲面，增加几何体的细节。"}],"\n",["$","li","li-2",{"children":"示例用途：实现平滑曲面或动态细分网格。"}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-5",{"children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":"着色器管线中的其他阶段"}],"\n",["$","ul","ul-0",{"children":["\n",["$","li","li-0",{"children":["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":"裁剪着色器（Clipping Shader）"}]}],"\n",["$","li","li-1",{"children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":"光线追踪着色器（Raytracing Shader）"}]," 等。"]}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}]

18:["$","h2","h2-1",{"id":"shader-的语言","children":"Shader 的语言"}]
19:["$","p","p-2",{"data-indent":"2em","children":"Shader 通常使用专门的语言编写，这些语言被设计为能够高效地在 GPU 上运行。例如："}]
1a:["$","ul","ul-1",{"children":["\n",["$","li","li-0",{"children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":"GLSL（OpenGL Shading Language）："}]," 用于 OpenGL。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-1",{"children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":"HLSL（High-Level Shading Language）："}]," 用于 DirectX。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-2",{"children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":"Cg（C for Graphics）："}]," NVIDIA 推出的语言。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-3",{"children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":"ShaderLab（Unity）："}]," Unity 的着色器语言，结合 HLSL 使用。"]}],"\n"]}]

1c:["$","p","p-3",{"data-indent":"2em","children":"GLSL 中的数据类型主要分为以下几类："}]
1d:["$","h3","h3-0",{"id":"1-标量类型scalar-types","children":["1. ",["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":"标量类型（Scalar Types）"}]]}]

1f:["$","ul","ul-2",{"children":["\n",["$","li","li-0",{"children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":["$","code","code-0",{"children":"float"}]}],"：表示单精度浮点数，范围通常为 ",["$","code","code-0",{"children":"±3.4 × 10^38"}],"，精度为 6-9 位数字。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-1",{"children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":["$","code","code-0",{"children":"int"}]}],"：表示整数，范围通常为 ",["$","code","code-0",{"children":"-2,147,483,648"}]," 到 ",["$","code","code-1",{"children":"2,147,483,647"}],"。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-2",{"children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":["$","code","code-0",{"children":"bool"}]}],"：布尔类型，取值为 ",["$","code","code-0",{"children":"true"}]," 或 ",["$","code","code-1",{"children":"false"}],"。"]}],"\n"]}]
20:["$","h3","h3-1",{"id":"2-向量类型vector-types","children":["2. ",["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":"向量类型（Vector Types）"}]]}]
21:["$","p","p-5",{"data-indent":"2em","children":"向量类型用于存储多个标量值，通常表示颜色、位置、法线等。GLSL 中有以下几种向量类型："}]
22:["$","ul","ul-3",{"children":["\n",["$","li","li-0",{"children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":["$","code","code-0",{"children":"vec2"}]}],"：包含两个浮点数或整数的向量，例如 ",["$","code","code-0",{"children":"(x, y)"}],"。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-1",{"children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":["$","code","code-0",{"children":"vec3"}]}],"：包含三个浮点数或整数的向量，例如 ",["$","code","code-0",{"children":"(x, y, z)"}],"。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-2",{"children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":["$","code","code-0",{"children":"vec4"}]}],"：包含四个浮点数或整数的向量，例如 ",["$","code","code-0",{"children":"(x, y, z, w)"}],"。"]}],"\n"]}]
23:["$","p","p-6",{"data-indent":"2em","children":["向量的元素可以是 ",["$","code","code-0",{"children":"float"}],"、",["$","code","code-1",{"children":"int"}]," 或 ",["$","code","code-2",{"children":"bool"}],"，例如 ",["$","code","code-3",{"children":"ivec2"}]," 表示两个整数的向量，",["$","code","code-4",{"children":"bvec4"}]," 表示四个布尔值的向量。"]}]

25:["$","p","p-7",{"data-indent":"2em","children":"矩阵类型用于表示线性变换，通常用于3D图形变换。GLSL支持以下矩阵类型："}]
26:["$","ul","ul-4",{"children":["\n",["$","li","li-0",{"children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":["$","code","code-0",{"children":"mat2"}]}],"：2x2 的浮点矩阵。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-1",{"children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":["$","code","code-0",{"children":"mat3"}]}],"：3x3 的浮点矩阵。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-2",{"children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":["$","code","code-0",{"children":"mat4"}]}],"：4x4 的浮点矩阵。"]}],"\n"]}]

35:["$","h2","h2-3",{"id":"glsl-的内置变量","children":"GLSL 的内置变量"}]
36:["$","h3","h3-7",{"id":"顶点着色器的内建变量","children":["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":"顶点着色器的内建变量"}]}]
37:["$","p","p-14",{"data-indent":"2em","children":"顶点着色器用于处理每个顶点的数据，其内建变量用于传递信息到图形管线的后续阶段。"}]
38:["$","ol","ol-1",{"children":["\n",["$","li","li-0",{"children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":"输入变量"}],"\n",["$","ul","ul-0",{"children":["\n",["$","li","li-0",{"children":[["$","code","code-0",{"children":"gl_VertexID"}],"：当前顶点的索引（整型）。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-1",{"children":[["$","code","code-0",{"children":"gl_InstanceID"}],"：当前实例的索引（用于实例化绘制）。"]}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-1",{"children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":"输出变量"}],"\n",["$","ul","ul-0",{"children":["\n",["$","li","li-0",{"children":[["$","code","code-0",{"children":"gl_Position"}],"：顶点的裁剪空间坐标，必须由顶点着色器设置。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-1",{"children":[["$","code","code-0",{"children":"gl_PointSize"}],"：绘制点图元时，指定点的大小（像素单位）。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-2",{"children":[["$","code","code-0",{"children":"gl_ClipDistance[]"}],"：用户定义的剪裁平面距离，用于实现自定义剪裁逻辑。"]}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}]

3a:["$","h3","h3-8",{"id":"片段着色器的内建变量","children":["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":"片段着色器的内建变量"}]}]
3b:["$","p","p-15",{"data-indent":"2em","children":"片段着色器用于处理每个片段的数据，内建变量帮助与栅格化阶段交互。"}]
3c:["$","ol","ol-2",{"children":["\n",["$","li","li-0",{"children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":"输入变量"}],"\n",["$","ul","ul-0",{"children":["\n",["$","li","li-0",{"children":[["$","code","code-0",{"children":"gl_FragCoord"}],"：片段在窗口空间的坐标（",["$","code","code-1",{"children":"x, y"}]," 为像素坐标，",["$","code","code-2",{"children":"z"}]," 为深度值，",["$","code","code-3",{"children":"w"}]," 为投影的倒数）。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-1",{"children":[["$","code","code-0",{"children":"gl_FrontFacing"}],"：布尔值，指示当前片段是否属于正面（面向摄像机的多边形）。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-2",{"children":[["$","code","code-0",{"children":"gl_PointCoord"}],"：在绘制点精灵时，提供片段在点图元中的归一化坐标。"]}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-1",{"children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"children":"输出变量"}],"\n",["$","ul","ul-0",{"children":["\n",["$","li","li-0",{"children":[["$","code","code-0",{"children":"gl_FragDepth"}],"：片段的深度值，可用于手动调整深度测试的行为。"]}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}]
